SELECT [t].[Id], [t].[ActionType], [t].[Code], [t].[CreatedDate], [t].[Definition], [t].[HttpType], [t].[MenuId], [t].[Name], [t].[Status], [t].[UpdatedDate], [t].[Id0], [t].[CreatedDate0], [t].[Name0], [t].[Status0], [t].[UpdatedDate0], [t0].[ActionsId], [t0].[RolesId], [t0].[Id], [t0].[ConcurrencyStamp], [t0].[CreatedDate], [t0].[Name], [t0].[NormalizedName]
FROM (
    SELECT TOP(1) [e].[Id], [e].[ActionType], [e].[Code], [e].[CreatedDate], [e].[Definition], [e].[HttpType], [e].[MenuId], [e].[Name], [e].[Status], [e].[UpdatedDate], [m].[Id] AS [Id0], [m].[CreatedDate] AS [CreatedDate0], [m].[Name] AS [Name0], [m].[Status] AS [Status0], [m].[UpdatedDate] AS [UpdatedDate0]

    INNER JOIN [Menus] AS [m] ON [e].[MenuId] = [m].[Id]
    WHERE ([e].[Code] = @__code_0) AND ([m].[Name] = @__menu_1)
) AS [t]

) AS [t0] ON [t].[Id] = [t0].[ActionsId]
ORDER BY [t].[Id], [t].[Id0], [t0].[ActionsId], [t0].[RolesId], [t0].[Id]
